    FROM [Tasks] AS [t4]

FROM [Projects] AS [p]
INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [p].[OwnerId] = [u].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Title], [t].[Description], [t].[Status], [t].[CreatedAt], [t].[DueDate], [t].[ProjectId], [p0].[Name], [p0].[Id] AS [Id0], [t0].[TaskId], [t0].[UserId], [t1].[UserId] AS [UserId0], [t1].[TaskId] AS [TaskId0], [t2].[TaskId] AS [TaskId1], [t2].[UserId] AS [UserId1], [s].[FullName], [s].[TaskId] AS [TaskId2], [s].[UserId] AS [UserId2], [s].[Id] AS [Id1]

    WHERE [p].[Id] = [t4].[ProjectId])
FROM [Projects] AS [p]
INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [p].[OwnerId] = [u].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Title], [t].[Description], [t].[Status], [t].[CreatedAt], [t].[DueDate], [t].[ProjectId], [p0].[Name], [p0].[Id] AS [Id0], [t0].[TaskId], [t0].[UserId], [t1].[UserId] AS [UserId0], [t1].[TaskId] AS [TaskId0], [t2].[TaskId] AS [TaskId1], [t2].[UserId] AS [UserId1], [s].[FullName], [s].[TaskId] AS [TaskId2], [s].[UserId] AS [UserId2], [s].[Id] AS [Id1]
    FROM [Tasks] AS [t]
    INNER JOIN [Projects] AS [p0] ON [t].[ProjectId] = [p0].[Id]
    LEFT JOIN [TaskAssignedUsers] AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[TaskId]
    LEFT JOIN [TaskAssignedUsers] AS [t1] ON [t].[Id] = [t1].[TaskId]

        INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u0] ON [t3].[UserId] = [u0].[Id]
    ) AS [s] ON [t].[Id] = [s].[TaskId]
) AS [s0] ON [p].[Id] = [s0].[ProjectId]
